This is the Carbon for IBM.com website, which includes documentation and guidelines around design and development for IBM.com

[www.ibm.com/standards/carbon/](https://www.ibm.com/standards/carbon/ "https://www.ibm.com/standards/carbon/")

Carbon for IBM.com Website
==========================

[](https://github.com/carbon-design-system/carbon-for-ibm-dotcom-website?screenshot=true#--carbon-for-ibmcom-website)

This is the Carbon for IBM.com website, which includes documentation and guidelines around design and development for IBM.com.

This is based on the [Gatsby Theme from Carbon](https://gatsby-theme-carbon.now.sh/).

Contributing
------------

[](https://github.com/carbon-design-system/carbon-for-ibm-dotcom-website?screenshot=true#contributing)

If you are a publisher and would like to make content changes, you can read more about how to contribute at [Contributing](https://github.com/carbon-design-system/carbon-for-ibm-dotcom-website/blob/main/.github/CONTRIBUTING.md)

Publishing
----------

[](https://github.com/carbon-design-system/carbon-for-ibm-dotcom-website?screenshot=true#publishing)

Changes are currently auto-published to [https://www.ibm.com/standards/carbon](https://www.ibm.com/standards/carbon) once changes are merged back to the `main` branch. Previews can also be viewed once a pull request is created.

Resources
---------

[](https://github.com/carbon-design-system/carbon-for-ibm-dotcom-website?screenshot=true#resources)

*   [Available Components for Authoring](https://gatsby-theme-carbon.now.sh/components/markdown)
*   [Markdown Cheatsheet](https://github.com/adam-p/markdown-here/wiki/Markdown-Cheatsheet)

About
-----

This is the Carbon for IBM.com website, which includes documentation and guidelines around design and development for IBM.com

[www.ibm.com/standards/carbon/](https://www.ibm.com/standards/carbon/ "https://www.ibm.com/standards/carbon/")
